}

	name = Lodos # Canon, priest who claimed to be Lodos reborn

	diplomacy = 6
	martial = 5
	stewardship = 4
	intrigue = 4
	prowess = 6

		add_character_flag = canon_status_canon
		effect = {
			if = { # Kill off character if the game is loaded before Lodos came back from dead
				limit = { game_start_date < 8037.9.9 }
				death = { death_reason = death_suicide }
			}
		}
	}
	8037.9.9 = { # Replaces Lodos
		effect = {
			clear_traits = yes
			copy_traits = character:Drowned_Men_3 # Lodos
			copy_inheritable_appearance_from = character:Drowned_Men_3 # Lodos
			change_first_name = Lodos
		}
	}
	8038.3.1 = {
		death = {
			death_reason = death_execution
			killer = Greyjoy_41 # Goren Greyjoy
		}
	}
}
